/**
SELECT 
    msc.name as category_name,
    ms.id as service_id,
    ms.name_en as service_name
FROM medical_services ms
JOIN medical_service_categories_relations mscr ON ms.id = mscr.medical_service_id
JOIN medical_service_categories msc ON mscr.medical_service_category_id = msc.id
ORDER BY msc.id, ms.name_en LIMIT 10000
*/
